---
layout: "post"
permalink: /stlc-agda/
title: "Simple Typed Lambda Calculus In Agda"
date: "2018-08-17"
categories: type-theory home
toc: true
agda: true
latex: true
home: false
---

We present a formalisation of the syntax in Agda for the *Simple Typed Lambda
Calculus (STLC)* with some of its properties and the description of the
type-checking for this type system. We refactor the implementation by
[@gergoerdi](https://github.com/gergoerdi/stlc-agda/) for this calculus,
in particular the [Scopecheck](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk/blob/master/src/Scopecheck.agda)
and [Typecheck](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk/blob/master/src/Typecheck.agda) module.

The following source code was tested with:

- Agda v2.5.4
- Agda Standard Library v0.16

The original content was firstly exposed in the seminar of logic at Universidad EAFIT.

  - [Slides](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk/raw/master/slides/slides.pdf).
  - Repository: [https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk](https://github.com/jonaprieto/stlctalk).

{: .foldable }

### Bound

Lambda terms using De Bruijn indexes.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2103" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Bound"></a><a id="2110" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2110" class="Module">Bound</a> <a id="2116" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2117" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2117" class="Bound">Type</a> <a id="2122" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2124" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="2127" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2129" class="Keyword">where</a>

Syntax using indexes.

      <a id="3192" class="Comment">------------------------------</a>
      <a id="3229" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3231" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3149" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="3233" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2783" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="3235" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1548" class="InductiveConstructor">lam</a> <a id="3239" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3240" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3138" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="3242" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1468" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∶</a> <a id="3244" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3140" class="Bound">A</a><a id="3245" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3247" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3142" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="3249" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2783" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="3251" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2487" class="InductiveConstructor">lam</a> <a id="3255" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3140" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3257" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#3144" class="Bound">t&#39;</a>

### Scopecheck

Check representation of λ-terms using de Bruijn indexes.
Get a λ-term using de Bruijn indexes by given a λ-term with names.

{: .foldable }
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="4331" class="Comment">-- ∃-syntax and ∄-syntax</a>

    <a id="5953" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5955" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5956" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5956" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="5958" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5960" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2657" class="Function">Binder</a> <a id="5967" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5946" class="Bound">n</a><a id="5968" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5970" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5972" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5973" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5973" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="5975" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5977" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1378" class="Function">Name</a><a id="5981" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="5987" class="Comment">------------------------------</a>
    <a id="6022" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6024" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#534" class="Datatype">Dec</a> <a id="6028" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6029" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4474" class="Function">∃[</a> <a id="6032" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6032" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="6034" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4474" class="Function">]</a> <a id="6036" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6037" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5956" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="6039" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2783" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="6041" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1524" class="InductiveConstructor">var</a> <a id="6045" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5973" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6047" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2783" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="6049" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6032" class="Bound">t</a><a id="6050" class="Symbol">))</a>

              <a id="6744" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="6749" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#5332" class="Function">name-dec</a> <a id="6758" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6718" class="Bound">Γ,y⊢varx⇝t</a>
            <a id="6781" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="6786" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6788" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#470" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="6793" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6793" class="Bound">x≡y</a>                    <a id="6816" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6818" class="Bound">x≢y</a> <a id="6822" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6793" class="Bound">x≡y</a>
            <a id="6838" class="Symbol">...</a>  <a id="6843" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6845" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#495" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="6850" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6850" class="Bound">p</a><a id="6851" class="Symbol">@(</a><a id="6853" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6853" class="Bound">t′</a> <a id="6856" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">-by-</a> <a id="6861" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6861" class="Bound">Γ⊢varx⇝t′</a><a id="6870" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6872" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6874" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6602" class="Bound">∄t⟨Γ⊢varx⇝t⟩</a> <a id="6887" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#6850" class="Bound">p</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We want to determine if given a variable context and a term,
it is possible to find its encoding using De Bruijn indexes.
If so, we got its respective construction for that lambda term.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Scopecheck.check"></a><a id="7103" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7103" class="Function">check</a>
    <a id="7113" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7115" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="7117" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7118" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7118" class="Bound">n</a><a id="7119" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="7125" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7127" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7128" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7128" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7130" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7132" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2657" class="Function">Binder</a> <a id="7139" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7118" class="Bound">n</a><a id="7140" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="7146" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7148" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7149" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7149" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="7151" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7153" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1503" class="Datatype">S.Expr</a><a id="7159" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="7165" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7167" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#534" class="Datatype">Dec</a> <a id="7171" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7172" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4474" class="Function">∃[</a> <a id="7175" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7175" class="Bound">t′</a> <a id="7178" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#4474" class="Function">]</a> <a id="7180" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7181" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7128" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7183" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2783" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="7185" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7149" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="7187" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2783" class="Datatype Operator">⇝</a> <a id="7189" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7175" class="Bound">t′</a><a id="7191" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="7197" class="Comment">-- By induction on the term syntax.</a>

  <a id="8723" class="Comment">-- Go from a representation that uses Names to one that uses de Bruijn indices</a>
  <a id="Scopecheck.scope"></a><a id="8804" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8804" class="Function">scope</a> <a id="8810" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8812" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8813" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8813" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="8815" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8817" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#1503" class="Datatype">S.Expr</a><a id="8823" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8825" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8827" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8828" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8828" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="8830" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8832" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Decidable.html#897" class="Function">True</a> <a id="8837" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8838" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#7103" class="Function">check</a> <a id="8844" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Vec.html#712" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a> <a id="8847" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8813" class="Bound">t</a><a id="8848" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="8851" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8853" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#2432" class="Datatype">Expr</a> <a id="8858" class="Number">0</a>
  <a id="8862" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8804" class="Function">scope</a> <a id="8868" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8868" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="8870" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8871" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8871" class="Bound">p</a><a id="8872" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8874" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8876" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#155" class="Field">proj₁</a> <a id="8882" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8883" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Decidable.html#1055" class="Function">toWitness</a> <a id="8893" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#8871" class="Bound">p</a><a id="8894" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

    <a id="10589" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10525" class="Function">K</a> <a id="10591" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10593" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9994" class="InductiveConstructor">tLam</a> <a id="10598" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10599" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9994" class="InductiveConstructor">tLam</a> <a id="10604" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9928" class="InductiveConstructor">tVar</a><a id="10608" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="10615" class="Keyword">postulate</a>
      <a id="Typing.A"></a><a id="10631" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10631" class="Postulate">A</a> <a id="10633" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10635" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9517" class="Datatype">Type</a>
      <a id="Typing.B"></a><a id="10646" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10646" class="Postulate">B</a> <a id="10648" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10650" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9517" class="Datatype">Type</a>
      <a id="Typing.C"></a><a id="10661" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#10661" class="Postulate">C</a> <a id="10663" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10665" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-08-17-notes-sltc.md %}{% raw %}#9517" class="Datatype">Type</a>

    <a id="10675" class="Comment">-- S : [] ⊢ lam (A ↣ (B ↣ C))</a>
    <a id="10709" class="Comment">--              (lam (A ↣ B)</a>
    <a id="10742" class="Comment">--                   (lam A</a>
    <a id="10774" class="Comment">--                     ((var (# 2)) ∙ (var (# 0))) ∙ ((var (# 1)) ∙ (var (# 0))) ))</a>
    <a id="10862" class="Comment">--        ∶ (A ↣ (B ↣ C)) ↣ (A ↣ B) ↣ A ↣ C</a>
    <a id="10910" class="Comment">-- S = tLam (tLam ((tLam ({! tVar  !} ∙ {!   !})) ∙ ({! tVar  !} ∙ {!   !}))) --  tLam (tLam (tLam ((tVar ∙ tVar) ∙ (tVar ∙ tVar))))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### References
